QAtlas.fetch вҖ” Method
fetch(::ToricCode, ::AnyonStatistics; type::Symbol) -> NamedTuple

Topological data of one of the four toric-code anyons or the e/m mutual braiding. The returned NamedTuple shape depends on type:

typeNamedTuple fields
:e(label = :e, statistics = :boson, self_phase = 0.0, quantum_dim = 1.0, fusion = (:e, :e) => :1)
:m(label = :m, statistics = :boson, self_phase = 0.0, quantum_dim = 1.0, fusion = (:m, :m) => :1)
:Оө(label = :Оө, statistics = :fermion, self_phase = ПҖ, quantum_dim = 1.0, fusion = (:Оө, :Оө) => :1)
:em_braiding(label = :em_braiding, mutual_phase = ПҖ, anyons = (:e, :m))

Bosons have self-statistics phase 0; the bound state Оө = e Г— m acquires the relative phase ПҖ from the mutual e/m braid, making it a fermion. The e/m mutual phase is ПҖ (ZвӮӮ "mutual semion") вҖ” a full braid of one around the other multiplies the wave function by exp(iПҖ) = вҲ’1. All quantum dimensions are 1 (Abelian theory).

Aliases: type = :epsilon is accepted as a synonym of :Оө.

Throws an ErrorException for any other type.

source
QAtlas.fetch вҖ” Method
fetch(::ToricCode, ::GroundStateDegeneracy, ::PBC; genus::Int = 1) -> Int

Ground-state degeneracy on a closed orientable surface of genus g,

GSD(g) = 4^g.

This is the dimension of HВ№(ОЈ_g; ZвӮӮ) вҠ— HВ№(ОЈ_g; ZвӮӮ) (logical Pauli-X and Pauli-Z operators, one independent pair per non-contractible cycle). The torus (g = 1) gives the canonical 4-fold degeneracy. The result is purely topological вҖ” it depends only on genus, not on J_e, J_m or the lattice size.

PBC is the appropriate boundary tag because GSD is meaningful only on a closed surface; on OBC / a disk the model has a unique ground state (no homologically non-trivial loops), so the OBC method is intentionally not registered.

source
QAtlas.fetch вҖ” Method
fetch(::ToricCode, ::GroundStateEnergyDensity, ::Infinite) -> Float64

Ground-state energy density ОөвӮҖ = вҲ’(J_e + J_m).

Closed-form: every stabilizer commutes with every other, so the ground state simultaneously saturates A_v = +1 вҲҖv and B_p = +1 вҲҖp. The energy contribution per (vertex + plaquette) unit cell is вҲ’J_e вҲ’ J_m.

source
QAtlas.fetch вҖ” Method
fetch(::ToricCode, ::MassGap, ::Infinite) -> Float64

Single-anyon excitation gap О” = 2В·min(J_e, J_m).

Flipping a single vertex stabilizer eigenvalue (creating an e charge) costs 2 J_e; flipping a single plaquette (creating an m flux) costs 2 J_m. The minimum-energy excitation is therefore 2В·min(J_e, J_m) вҖ” the gap of the cheaper anyon species.

source
QAtlas.fetch вҖ” Method
fetch(::ToricCode, ::TopologicalEntanglementEntropy, ::Infinite) -> Float64

Topological entanglement entropy Оі = log 2.

For the ZвӮӮ topological order realised by the toric code, the total quantum dimension is рқ’ҹ = вҲҡ(ОЈ_a d_aВІ) = вҲҡ(1ВІ + 1ВІ + 1ВІ + 1ВІ) = 2 (four Abelian anyons {1, e, m, Оө}, each with d_a = 1). The KitaevвҖ“Preskill (2006) / LevinвҖ“Wen (2006) prescription extracts Оі = log рқ’ҹ = log 2 from the constant offset of the bipartite entanglement entropy on a simply-connected region,

S(ПҒ_A) = Оұ |вҲӮA| вҲ’ Оі + O(|вҲӮA|вҒ»В№).

Independent of J_e, J_m (purely topological).

Example

julia> QAtlas.fetch(ToricCode(), TopologicalEntanglementEntropy(), Infinite())
0.6931471805599453

QAtlas.fetch вҖ” Method
fetch(::TricriticalPotts3, ::ConformalWeights, ::Infinite; r::Integer, s::Integer, kwargs...)
    -> Rational{Int}

Conformal weight h_{r,s} from the Kac table of the tricritical 3-state Potts CFT, delegated to MinimalModel(7, 6):

h_{r,s}(p, p_prime) = ((p r - p_prime s)ВІ - (p - p_prime)ВІ) / (4 p p_prime),

with (p, p_prime) = (7, 6) in QAtlas' p > p_prime convention.

Index ranges follow MinimalModel: 1 вүӨ r вүӨ p_prime - 1 = 5 and 1 вүӨ s вүӨ p - 1 = 6. Returns Rational{Int}.

Examples:

  • h_{1,1} = 0 (identity, lowest weight)
  • h_{1,2} = 1/7 (energy operator Оө)
  • h_{2,1} = 3/8 (M(7,6) Kac (2,1))

References

  • A. A. Belavin, A. M. Polyakov, A. B. Zamolodchikov, Nucl. Phys. B 241, 333 (1984).
  • G. E. Andrews, R. J. Baxter, P. J. Forrester, J. Stat. Phys. 35, 193 (1984).

QAtlas.fetch вҖ” Method
fetch(::Universality{:Heisenberg}, ::CentralCharge; d::Int=1) -> Rational{Int}

Central charge of the spin-1/2 Heisenberg universality class.

Only d = 1 is supported (the spin-1/2 antiferromagnetic Heisenberg chain in the SU(2)_1 Wess-Zumino-Witten universality class, central charge c = 1). For d вүҘ 2 the Heisenberg universality class is not a 1+1D CFT (the 2D Heisenberg model has Goldstone modes; the 3D one has no critical line at finite T) вҖ” call sites that want a generic-CFT entanglement formula must use a 1+1D class.

Reference: AffleckвҖ“Haldane, Phys. Rev. B 36, 5291 (1987); di FrancescoвҖ“ MathieuвҖ“SГ©nГ©chal В§15.6 (SU(2)_1 WZW).

QAtlas.fetch вҖ” Method
fetch(::Universality{:KPZ}, ::GrowthExponents; d) -> NamedTuple

Scaling exponents of the KPZ universality class.

  • d = 1 (1+1D): all three exponents are exact Rational{Int}. Scaling relations: $Оұ + z = 2$ (Galilean invariance), $ОІ = Оұ / z$.

  • d = 2 (2+1D): numerical estimates from PagnaniвҖ“Parisi 2015 (large-scale RSOS simulations). Returns Float64 fields with _err companions: ОІ_growth = 0.2415(15), Оұ_rough = 0.393(5), z = 1.613(9).

  • d = 3 (3+1D): numerical estimates from KellingвҖ“Г“dor 2011 (octahedron model on GPU). Returns Float64 fields with _err companions: ОІ_growth вүҲ 0.18, Оұ_rough вүҲ 0.31, z вүҲ 1.51. Galilean invariance $Оұ + z = 2$ is not strictly satisfied by these estimates вҖ” the discrepancy reflects estimation uncertainty (and ongoing debate about whether KPZ has an upper critical dimension) rather than a violation of the symmetry. Treat the d=3 entry as best-numerical, not as a sharp reference.

Higher dimensions (d вүҘ 4) are not implemented; the upper critical dimension of KPZ remains an open problem.

QAtlas.fetch вҖ” Method
fetch(::Universality{:RMT}, ::SpectralFormFactor; ensemble::Symbol=:GUE, П„::Real=Inf) -> Float64

Disorder-averaged spectral form factor K(П„) for the random-matrix universality class in the large-N thermodynamic limit, with П„ = t / N (Heisenberg time П„_H = 2ПҖ).

QAtlas Phase 1 (issue #243) exposes only the GUE ensemble in the late-time plateau regime П„ вүҘ 2ПҖ, where the disorder-averaged SFF saturates universally to K(П„вҶ’вҲһ) = 1 (Mehta 2004 В§16; Cotler et al. 2017, arXiv:1611.04650).

The Mehta connection formula K(П„) = (П„/(2ПҖ)) вҲ’ (П„/(4ПҖ)) log|1 вҲ’ П„/(2ПҖ)| on the ramp side П„ < 2ПҖ, and the GOE / GSE sigma-model closed forms, are deferred to Phase 2.

Errors

  • DomainError if ensemble вү  :GUE (GOE / GSE Phase 2).
  • DomainError if П„ < 2ПҖ (ramp regime, Phase 2).

QAtlas.fetch вҖ” Method
fetch(::Universality{:RMT}, ::TracyWidom; ОІ::Int, x::Real) -> Float64

Tracy-Widom CDF F_ОІ(x) = P[Оҫ_ОІ вүӨ x] for ОІ вҲҲ {1, 2, 4} (GOE, GUE, GSE largest-eigenvalue limit law).

QAtlas Phase 1 evaluates F_ОІ from a tabulated grid compiled from Bornemann, On the numerical evaluation of Fredholm determinants, Math. Comp. 79, 871 (2010), Table 1; the table covers x вҲҲ [-4.0, 4.0] for all three ОІ. Inside the table support the interpolant is piecewise-linear and monotone non-decreasing. Outside the table the function returns the Tracy-Widom 1994/1996 left/right tail asymptotics, matched continuously to the table boundary.

Reference checkpoints (Bornemann 2010, Table 1):

  • F_1(0) вүҲ 0.8319
  • F_2(0) вүҲ 0.9694
  • F_4(0) вүҲ 0.99966

A direct PainlevГ©-II integrator (DifferentialEquations.jl based) is deferred to Phase 2; see issue #151.

QAtlas.fetch вҖ” Method
fetch(::Universality{:RMT}, ::WignerSurmise; ОІ::Int, s::Real) -> Float64

Wigner surmise nearest-neighbour level-spacing distribution P_ОІ(s) for ОІ вҲҲ {1, 2, 4}.

Closed-form expressions (mean spacing normalised to 1):

  • P_1(s) = (ПҖ s / 2) exp(-ПҖ sВІ / 4) GOE
  • P_2(s) = (32 sВІ / ПҖВІ) exp(-4 sВІ / ПҖ) GUE
  • P_4(s) = (2В№вҒё sвҒҙ / (3вҒ¶ ПҖВі)) exp(-64 sВІ / (9ПҖ)) GSE

Each integrates to 1 with first moment 1 (verified analytically and by the standalone test). Behaves as P_ОІ(s) ~ s^ОІ for s вҶ’ 0вҒә (level repulsion) and as P_ОІ(s) ~ exp(-c_ОІ sВІ) for large s.

Site-local energy density Оө_i of the OBC XXZ chain at inverse temperature beta, defined so that ОЈбөў Оө_i = вҹЁHвҹ©_ОІ. Each bond b_{i,i+1} = (J/4)(ПғЛЈПғЛЈ + ПғКёПғКё + О” Пғб¶»Пғб¶») is split symmetrically between its two endpoints:

QAtlas.fetch вҖ” Method
fetch(model::XXZ1D, ::Energy{:per_site}, ::Infinite; [beta]) -> Float64

Per-site energy of the infinite XXZ chain.

  • Without beta: ground-state energy density. Closed-form values at the three canonical points О” вҲҲ {-1, 0, 1}; warns and returns NaN otherwise (general-О” Bethe ansatz is a follow-up).

  • With beta: thermal energy density вҹЁHвҹ©_ОІ / N. At О” = 0 evaluated by Gauss-Kronrod quadrature of the free-fermion integral

    e(ОІ) = -(1/(2ПҖ)) вҲ«вӮҖ^ПҖ Оө(k) tanh(ОІ Оө(k) / 2) dk,   Оө(k) = -J cos k.

    The ОІ вҶ’ вҲһ limit reproduces -J/ПҖ (matching XXZ.jl's _xxz1d_energy_free_fermion). At general О” the thermal Bethe ansatz (issue #108) is required; a warning is emitted and NaN returned.

QAtlas.fetch вҖ” Method
fetch(model::XXZ1D, ::Energy{:total}, ::OBC; beta) -> Float64

Total thermal energy вҹЁHвҹ©_ОІ for the spin-ВҪ OBC chain at finite size, computed by dense ED. Works for any О” and any N вүӨ 12. Intended as a reference for MPS thermal methods (TPQMPS / Purification / METTS).

    вҹЁHвҹ©_ОІ = Tr(H exp(-ОІH)) / Tr(exp(-ОІH))

Convention matches fetch(::TFIM, ::Energy, ::OBC): finite-size boundary conditions return total energy; only Infinite() returns per-site (вҹЁHвҹ©/N, the only finite quantity in the thermodynamic limit).

source
QAtlas.fetch вҖ” Method
fetch(model::XXZ1D, ::FreeEnergy, ::Infinite; beta::Real, kwargs...)

Per-site Helmholtz free energy of the infinite XXZ chain. Currently only О” = 0 (XX / free fermion) is implemented:

f(ОІ) = -(1/(ПҖОІ)) вҲ«вӮҖ^ПҖ log(2 cosh(ОІ Оө(k) / 2)) dk,   Оө(k) = -J cos k.

For other О” the thermal Bethe ansatz (issue #108) is required; this method emits a warning and returns NaN.

source
QAtlas.fetch вҖ” Method
fetch(model_f::XXZ1D, ::LoschmidtEcho{:rate}, ::Infinite;
      initial::XXZ1D, t::Real) -> Float64

Loschmidt rate function

О»(t) = - lim_{NвҶ’вҲһ} (1/N) log |вҹЁПҲвӮҖ | e^{-iH_f t} | ПҲвӮҖвҹ©|ВІ

for the XX вҶ’ XX quench H_XX(JвӮҖ) вҶ’ H_XX(J_f) of the infinite О” = 0 chain (Calabrese-Essler-Fagotti, J. Stat. Mech. (2012) P07016, specialised to the Gaussian-state-to-Gaussian-state, no-pairing sub-case).

Because H_XX(J) JordanвҖ“Wigner-transforms to a tight-binding fermion chain without pairing, both H_XX(JвӮҖ) and H_XX(J_f) are diagonalised in the same plane-wave basis c(k). The Loschmidt amplitude therefore factorises into single-mode phases,

вҹЁПҲвӮҖ | e^{-iH_f t} | ПҲвӮҖвҹ©
  = вҲҸ_k exp{ -i Оө_{J_f}(k) t В· (n_k(JвӮҖ) - 1/2) },

whose modulus is identically 1 (each factor is a pure phase). Equivalently, |ПҲвӮҖвҹ© = |GS(JвӮҖ)вҹ© is a number eigenstate of H_f because both Hamiltonians are diagonal in the same {nМӮ_k}, so e^{-iH_f t}|ПҲвӮҖвҹ© = e^{-iE_f^{(JвӮҖ)} t}|ПҲвӮҖвҹ© is a pure phase. Hence

О»(t) вүЎ 0          for every (JвӮҖ, J_f), including sgn JвӮҖ вү  sgn J_f.

The static overlap |вҹЁGS(JвӮҖ)|GS(J_f)вҹ©| does vanish at sign-flip (Anderson orthogonality of complementary Fermi seas), but that is a different quantity from the Loschmidt autocorrelation and does not enter О»(t).

This trivial result holds because the only XX вҶ’ XX quench expressible in the current XXZ1D model class is GS-to-GS without any Bogoliubov-rotation knob. A non-trivial Loschmidt rate appears in quenches from non-Gaussian initial states (NГ©el / dimer; CEF 2012) or under XY-pairing dynamics, both of which are Phase-2 follow-ups (see issues #143, #146).

Arguments

  • model_f::XXZ1D вҖ” final Hamiltonian. Must have О” = 0 (otherwise DomainError); a follow-up issue (#108 / #143) covers О” вү  0.
  • initial::XXZ1D вҖ” initial Hamiltonian whose ground state is the pre-quench state |ПҲвӮҖвҹ©. Must also have О” = 0.
  • t::Real вҖ” real evolution time.

Returns

0.0 (the trivial Phase-1 value, valid for every t вүҘ 0 and every sign combination of (initial.J, model_f.J)).

Examples

julia> m = XXZ1D(; J=1.0, О”=0.0);

julia> fetch(m, LoschmidtEcho(; mode=:rate), Infinite(); initial=m, t=1.0)
0.0

julia> fetch(m, LoschmidtEcho(; mode=:rate), Infinite();
             initial=XXZ1D(; J=0.5, О”=0.0), t=1.0)
0.0

julia> fetch(m, LoschmidtEcho(; mode=:rate), Infinite();
             initial=XXZ1D(; J=-1.0, О”=0.0), t=1.0)   # sign-flip вҖ” also 0
0.0

References

  • P. Calabrese, F.H.L. Essler, M. Fagotti, J. Stat. Mech. (2012) P07016 вҖ” XX-quench dynamics, Loschmidt amplitude.
  • M. Heyl, A. Polkovnikov, S. Kehrein, Phys. Rev. Lett. 110, 135704 (2013) вҖ” definition of the dynamical Loschmidt rate О»(t).
  • F.H.L. Essler, M. Fagotti, J. Stat. Mech. (2016) 064002.

QAtlas.fetch вҖ” Method

Per-site bulk magnetisation вҹЁОЈбөў Пғб¶»бөўвҹ©_ОІ / N. ОЈбөў Пғб¶»бөў commutes with H (U(1) symmetry), so the thermal average is Tr(M_z exp(-ОІH))/Z; for even N and any real ОІ the Пғб¶»-product basis groups symmetrically between sectors of opposite total Sб¶» and the average is zero. For odd N the unique smallest-Sб¶»-magnitude sector is half-filled ВұВҪ (still S_z = ВұВҪ), so the average is again zero up to round-off.

source
QAtlas.fetch вҖ” Method
fetch(m::XYh1D, ::Energy{:per_site}, ::Infinite;
      Jx=m.Jx, Jy=m.Jy, h=m.h, kwargs...) -> Float64

Ground-state energy per site of the LSM/Pfeuty XY chain in a transverse field, restricted to the isotropic XX limit Jx = Jy = J. Via Jordan-Wigner the model maps to free spinless fermions with single-particle dispersion Оҫ(k) = 2h вҲ’ 4J cos k; the ground state fills all modes with Оҫ(k) < 0.

In the thermodynamic limit, with the LSM 1961 sign convention H = вҲ’J ОЈ(ПғЛЈПғЛЈ + ПғКёПғКё) вҲ’ h ОЈ Пғб¶»,

  • h вүҘ 2J (empty Fermi sea, all spins вҶ‘): E/N = вҲ’h

  • h вүӨ вҲ’2J (full Fermi sea, all spins вҶ“): E/N = h

  • |h| < 2J (partially filled, k_F = arccos(h/2J)):

    E/N = вҲ’h + (2h/ПҖ) В· arccos(h/(2J))
          вҲ’ (4J/ПҖ) В· вҲҡ(1 вҲ’ (h/(2J))ВІ).

At h = 0: E/N = вҲ’4J/ПҖ вүҲ вҲ’1.27323954J (Lieb-Schultz-Mattis 1961).

Anisotropic Jx вү  Jy raises DomainError вҖ” Phase 2.

References

  • E. Lieb, T. Schultz, D. Mattis, Annals Phys. 16, 407 (1961).
  • P. Pfeuty, Annals Phys. 57, 79 (1970).
source
QAtlas.fetch вҖ” Method
fetch(m::XYh1D, ::MassGap, ::Infinite;
      Jx=m.Jx, Jy=m.Jy, h=m.h, kwargs...) -> Float64

Single-particle Bogoliubov gap of the LSM/Pfeuty XY chain in a transverse field, restricted to the isotropic XX limit Jx = Jy = J. In that limit the dispersion collapses to Оө(k) = |h вҲ’ 2J cos k|, and the gap closes whenever |h| вүӨ 2J:

MassGap = 2 В· max(0, |h| вҲ’ 2J).

Anisotropic Jx вү  Jy raises DomainError вҖ” Phase 2.

References

  • E. Lieb, T. Schultz, D. Mattis, Annals Phys. 16, 407 (1961).
  • P. Pfeuty, Annals Phys. 57, 79 (1970).

QAtlas.fetch вҖ” Method
fetch(::YangLee, ::ConformalWeights, ::Infinite; r::Integer=1, s::Integer=1, kwargs...)
    -> Rational{Int}

Kac-formula conformal weight h_{r,s} of the Yang-Lee CFT, delegated to MinimalModel(5, 2).

For M(p, pprime) = M(5, 2) the Kac-table index range is `r вҲҲ [1, pprime - 1] = [1, 1](onlyr = 1) ands вҲҲ [1, p - 1] = [1, 4], with the Kac symmetry(r, s) вҶ” (p_prime - r, p - s)` identifying

(1, 1) вҶ” (1, 4)   with   h = 0           (identity)
(1, 2) вҶ” (1, 3)   with   h = -1/5         (Yang-Lee primary)

so the theory has only two distinct primaries.

Out-of-range (r, s) throws DomainError (inherited from MinimalModel).

References

  • J. L. Cardy, Phys. Rev. Lett. 54, 1354 (1985).

QAtlas.fetch вҖ” Method
fetch(m::ZnClock, ::CentralCharge, ::Infinite; n::Integer=m.n, kwargs...)
    -> Rational{Int}

Central charge of the 2-D Z_n clock model, currently supported for n = 2 and n = 3 via delegation:

  • n = 2: MinimalModel(4, 3) вҶ’ c = 1/2 (Ising universality).
  • n = 3: MinimalModel(6, 5) вҶ’ c = 4/5 (3-state Potts universality).

For n = 4 (Ashkin-Teller line) and n вүҘ 5 (intermediate BKT phase) the critical theory is a continuous family of c = 1 CFTs and selecting a particular member requires a coupling; those branches throw a DomainError and are deferred to Phase 2.

References

  • J. V. JosГ©, L. P. Kadanoff, S. Kirkpatrick, D. R. Nelson, Phys. Rev. B 16, 1217 (1977).
  • S. Elitzur, R. B. Pearson, J. Shigemitsu, Phys. Rev. D 19, 3698 (1979).

QAtlas.fetch вҖ” Method
fetch(::ZnParafermion, ::CentralCharge, ::Infinite; n=m.n) -> Rational{Int}

Central charge of the Z_n parafermion CFT (Fateev-Zamolodchikov 1985):

c(n) = 2(n - 1) / (n + 2)

equivalent to the SU(2)_n / U(1) coset central charge. Special values:

  • n = 2 вҶ’ c = 1/2 (Ising / Majorana)
  • n = 3 вҶ’ c = 4/5 (3-state Potts)
  • n = 4 вҶ’ c = 1 (compactified free boson)
  • n = 5 вҶ’ c = 8/7
  • n вҶ’ вҲһ вҶ’ c вҶ’ 2 (asymptotic SU(2) WZW level вҶ’ вҲһ)

Returned as an exact Rational{Int}.

References

  • V. A. Fateev, A. B. Zamolodchikov, Sov. Phys. JETP 62, 215 (1985).

CalabreseвҖ“Cardy RГ©nyi-Оұ entanglement entropy in the thermodynamic limit, L вҶ’ вҲһ:

S_Оұ(в„“) = ((c/6)(1 + 1/Оұ)) В· log в„“.

QAtlas.fetch вҖ” Method
fetch(::Universality{C}, ::RenyiEntropy, ::OBC; в„“::Real, L::Real, kwargs...)

CalabreseвҖ“Cardy RГ©nyi-Оұ entanglement entropy on an open chain. Same closed form as the von Neumann OBC case with the substitution

c -> c В· (1 + 1/Оұ) / 2,

so

S_Оұ(в„“, L) = ((c/12)(1 + 1/Оұ)) В· log[(2L/ПҖ) sin(ПҖв„“/L)].

The non-universal c'_1 and AffleckвҖ“Ludwig log g are dropped.

QAtlas.fetch вҖ” Method

CalabreseвҖ“Cardy RГ©nyi-Оұ entanglement entropy on a periodic chain. Same closed form as the von Neumann case with the substitution

c -> c В· (1 + 1/Оұ) / 2,

i.e.

S_Оұ(в„“, L) = ((c/6)(1 + 1/Оұ)) В· log[(L/ПҖ) sin(ПҖв„“/L)]

Reduces to the von Neumann result at Оұ = 1 (which is excluded here because RenyiEntropy(1) throws вҖ” use VonNeumannEntropy() instead).

QAtlas.fetch вҖ” Method
fetch(::Universality{C}, ::VonNeumannEntropy, ::Infinite; в„“::Real, kwargs...)
    -> Float64

CalabreseвҖ“Cardy von Neumann entanglement entropy in the thermodynamic limit (L вҶ’ вҲһ) of a 1+1D CFT, with PBC scaling вҖ” i.e. two entanglement cuts in an infinite chain:

S(в„“) = (c/3) log в„“                                   (Infinite)

The non-universal additive constant is dropped. This is the standard "infinite-chain" reference used to extract the central charge from finite-size lattice data.

Reference: CalabreseвҖ“Cardy J. Stat. Mech. P06002 (2004) eq. (3.13).

source
QAtlas.fetch вҖ” Method
fetch(::Universality{C}, ::VonNeumannEntropy, ::OBC; в„“::Real, L::Real, kwargs...)
    -> Float64

CalabreseвҖ“Cardy von Neumann entanglement entropy on an open chain of length L, for the canonical "block at one boundary" geometry: the subsystem A occupies sites 1..в„“ (or equivalently L-в„“+1..L), so exactly one of A's endpoints sits at the open boundary and only one entanglement cut lies in the bulk:

S(в„“, L) = (c/6) log[(2L/ПҖ) sin(ПҖв„“/L)]                (OBC, block at end)

For a block in the bulk of an open chain (e.g. sites L/4..L/4+в„“ with both endpoints away from the boundary), there are two bulk cuts and the prefactor reverts to c/3, with a different log argument involving conformal cross-ratios of four points (CalabreseвҖ“ Cardy J. Phys. A 42, 504005 (2009) В§3.3). This bulk-block formula is not implemented by this method.

The non-universal additive constant c'_1 and the AffleckвҖ“Ludwig boundary entropy log g (boundary state-dependent) are dropped. At the balanced bipartition (в„“ = L/2) the OBC value is half of the PBC value (one entanglement cut vs two).

Reference: CalabreseвҖ“Cardy J. Stat. Mech. P06002 (2004) eq. (3.16); J. Phys. A 42, 504005 (2009) eq. (30). AffleckвҖ“Ludwig boundary entropy: AffleckвҖ“Ludwig, Phys. Rev. Lett. 67, 161 (1991).

source
QAtlas.fetch вҖ” Method
fetch(::Universality{C}, ::VonNeumannEntropy, ::PBC; в„“::Real, L::Real, kwargs...)
    -> Float64

CalabreseвҖ“Cardy von Neumann entanglement entropy of a contiguous block of length в„“ in a 1+1D CFT on a periodic chain of length L:

S(в„“, L) = (c/3) log[(L/ПҖ) sin(ПҖв„“/L)]                 (PBC)

The non-universal additive constant c'_1 (UV cutoff) is dropped. The central charge is fetched via fetch(Universality{C}(), CentralCharge()); classes without a 1+1D-CFT central charge raise ErrorException.

Boundary cases:

  • в„“ вҶ’ 0 or в„“ вҶ’ L: argument of the log вҶ’ 0, returns -Inf (UV divergence) вҖ” physically the cut runs through zero sites.
  • в„“ = L/2: maximum.

Reference: CalabreseвҖ“Cardy J. Stat. Mech. P06002 (2004) eq. (3.8); J. Phys. A 42, 504005 (2009) eq. (28).

source

QAtlas.has_native_fetch вҖ” Method
has_native_fetch(impl::Implementation) -> Bool

true iff which(fetch, (impl.model, impl.quantity, impl.bc)) resolves to a method more specific than the catch-all in core/type.jl. Conversion fallbacks (e.g. the generic Energy{:per_site} вҶ” Energy{:total} router) count as "native" because they are a real dispatchable implementation вҖ” they just live above the model layer.

Used by test/core/test_registry.jl to detect registry rows that silently lost their backing fetch method.

source
QAtlas.heisenberg_spinon_dispersion вҖ” Method
heisenberg_spinon_dispersion(model::Heisenberg1D, k::Real; J::Real = 1.0)
    -> Float64

Single-spinon dispersion of the spin-ВҪ antiferromagnetic Heisenberg chain in the thermodynamic limit (FaddeevвҖ“Takhtajan 1981):

Оө(k) = (ПҖ J / 2) |sin k|,   k вҲҲ [0, ПҖ].

Spinons are massless half-odd-integer-spin excitations and the lower edge of the two-spinon continuum coincides with this dispersion, see heisenberg_two_spinon_lower_edge.

Special values:

  • Оө(0) = 0 вҖ” gapless point.
  • Оө(ПҖ/2) = ПҖ J / 2 вҖ” band centre maximum.
  • Оө(ПҖ) = 0 вҖ” gapless Umklapp point.

J is passed by keyword because Heisenberg1D is parameterless in this codebase (every other quantity threads J through kwargs the same way).

References

L. D. Faddeev, L. A. Takhtajan, "What is the spin of a spin wave?",
  Phys. Lett. A 85, 375 (1981).
source
QAtlas.heisenberg_two_spinon_lower_edge вҖ” Method
heisenberg_two_spinon_lower_edge(model::Heisenberg1D, q::Real;
                                 J::Real = 1.0) -> Float64

Lower edge of the two-spinon continuum at total momentum q for the spin-ВҪ XXX AFM chain (des CloizeauxвҖ“Pearson 1962):

Оө_L(q) = (ПҖ J / 2) |sin q|.

By construction Оө_L(q) вүЎ Оө(q) where Оө is the single-spinon dispersion (heisenberg_spinon_dispersion) вҖ” this reflects the kinematic configuration in which one of the two spinons sits at zero energy, so the total energy equals the energy of the other.

Special values:

  • Оө_L(0) = Оө_L(ПҖ) = 0 вҖ” gapless points (Umklapp included).
  • Оө_L(ПҖ/2) = ПҖ J / 2 вҖ” maximum of the lower edge.

References

J. des Cloizeaux, J. J. Pearson, "Spin-wave spectrum of the
  antiferromagnetic linear chain", Phys. Rev. 128, 2131 (1962).
source
QAtlas.heisenberg_two_spinon_upper_edge вҖ” Method
heisenberg_two_spinon_upper_edge(model::Heisenberg1D, q::Real;
                                 J::Real = 1.0) -> Float64

Upper edge of the two-spinon continuum at total momentum q for the spin-ВҪ XXX AFM chain (des CloizeauxвҖ“Pearson 1962):

Оө_U(q) = ПҖ J |sin(q/2)|.

Special values:

  • Оө_U(0) = 0 вҖ” Goldstone-like vanishing of the support window at q = 0.
  • Оө_U(ПҖ) = ПҖ J вҖ” top of the continuum at the Umklapp point.

For q вҲҲ (0, ПҖ] one has Оө_U(q) вүҘ Оө_L(q) strictly except at the gapless points where the continuum collapses to a line.

References

J. des Cloizeaux, J. J. Pearson, "Spin-wave spectrum of the
  antiferromagnetic linear chain", Phys. Rev. 128, 2131 (1962).

QAtlas.implementation_status вҖ” Method
implementation_status() -> Vector{NamedTuple}
implementation_status(model::AbstractQAtlasModel)
implementation_status(::Type{<:AbstractQAtlasModel})
implementation_status(quantity::AbstractQuantity)
implementation_status(::Type{<:AbstractQuantity})
implementation_status(queue::AbstractVector)

Return registry rows as NamedTuples (Tables.jl-compatible without a Tables dependency).

  • No-arg: every registered triple.
  • model / quantity (instance or type): rows whose corresponding type field matches exactly (no subtype walking вҖ” model parameters are part of the identity here).
  • queue: a vector of (model, quantity, bc) triples (each component may be either an instance or a type). Returns one row per queue entry that is registered, dropping entries that are not.

Use this to plan downstream work вҖ” e.g. before writing tests for a new ThermalMPS workload, query the queue you intend to validate against.

Render entries (any iterable of NamedTuple rows from implementation_status) as a GitHub-flavoured Markdown table to io.

QAtlas.kdp_model вҖ” Method
kdp_model(a::Real) -> SixVertex

KDP model sub-family a free, b = c = 1 (Lieb 1967c). Phase boundary at a = 2:

  • a < 2 вҖ” disordered (О” вҲҲ (-1/2, 1) for 0 < a < 2).
  • a = 2 вҖ” critical (О” = 1).
  • a > 2 вҖ” ferroelectric, frozen (О” > 1, free energy вҲ’log a).

The "KDP" naming is historical (Slater's potassium-dihydrogen-phosphate ferroelectric model).

References

  • E. H. Lieb, Phys. Rev. Lett. 19, 108 (1967c).
source
QAtlas.native_energy_granularity вҖ” Function
native_energy_granularity(model, bc) -> :total | :per_site

Trait declaring which granularity the given model returns natively for Energy at boundary condition bc. Used by the Energy() (:natural) router and by the generic conversion fallbacks.

Every model that supports Energy must add a method per supported BC, e.g.

QAtlas.native_energy_granularity(::TFIM, ::OBC) = :total
QAtlas.native_energy_granularity(::TFIM, ::Infinite) = :per_site

A missing method is caught at the call site as a MethodError, which is intentional: it forces new models to declare the convention rather than silently inheriting an unrelated default.

source
QAtlas.native_energy_granularity вҖ” Method
native_energy_granularity(::S1Heisenberg1D, ::Infinite) -> :per_site

The infinite spin-1 Heisenberg chain has a well-defined per-site ground-state energy density eвӮҖ вүҲ -1.401484 J (White-Huse 1993) but no finite total energy. Per-site is the only meaningful granularity.

source
QAtlas.pfaffian вҖ” Method
pfaffian(A::AbstractMatrix) -> eltype(A)

Compute the Pfaffian of an antisymmetric matrix A.

A must be square of even dimension. Antisymmetry (A[i,j] == -A[j,i]) is assumed; only the strictly upper (or lower) triangle is semantically used вҖ” diagonal entries are ignored.

For an odd-dimensional antisymmetric matrix the Pfaffian is zero by definition, and that is returned.

Works for both real and complex numeric element types. The algorithm is numerically stable with partial pivoting and runs in O(nВі).

QAtlas.square_ice вҖ” Method
square_ice() -> SixVertex

Square-ice point a = b = c = 1 (О” = 1/2, disordered phase). The zero-temperature configurational entropy per vertex is the Lieb 1967a closed form

S/N = (3/2) log(4/3) вүҲ 0.4315231087вҖҰ

References

  • E. H. Lieb, Phys. Rev. 162, 162 (1967a).
source
QAtlas.tfim_quasiparticle_dispersion вҖ” Method
tfim_quasiparticle_dispersion(model::TFIM, k::Real) -> Float64

Single-quasiparticle Bogoliubov dispersion of the infinite TFIM,

Оӣ(k) = 2 вҲҡ(JВІ + hВІ вҲ’ 2 J h cos k),

at momentum k вҲҲ [0, ПҖ]. Useful for plotting band structure and as the kinematic input to two-spinon density-of-states / structure factor calculations.

Special values:

  • Оӣ(0) = 2 |J вҲ’ h| вҖ” equal to the gap О” in either phase.
  • Оӣ(ПҖ) = 2 (J + h) вҖ” top of the band.
  • min over k вҲҲ [0, ПҖ] is the mass gap MassGap at Infinite.
source
QAtlas.tfim_two_spinon_dos вҖ” Method
tfim_two_spinon_dos(model::TFIM, Пү::Real; q_total::Real = 0.0) -> Float64

Two-spinon density of states at total momentum q_total and frequency Пү for the infinite TFIM:

ПҒ_2(Пү; q_total) = (1/ПҖ) вҲ«вӮҖ^ПҖ dk  Оҙ(Пү вҲ’ Оӣ(k) вҲ’ Оӣ(q_total вҲ’ k)).

For q_total = 0 the two-spinon continuum is supported on [2 О”, Оӣ(0) + Оӣ(ПҖ)] = [2 |J вҲ’ h|, 2 (J + h)]; outside this window the routine returns 0.0.

Computation: numerical root-finding for k* вҲҲ (0, ПҖ) where f(k) := Оӣ(k) + Оӣ(q_total вҲ’ k) = Пү, then

ПҒ_2(Пү; q_total) = (1/ПҖ) ОЈ_{k*} 1 / |f'(k*)|.

Roots are isolated by a brute-force scan with Nscan = 4096 samples followed by 50 bisection refinements per bracket вҖ” sufficient for ~12-digit precision in k* and ~1/Nscan precision in counting roots near van Hove singularities (where |f'| vanishes and ПҒ_2 diverges integrably). Right at a van Hove point the returned value is finite because the bisected k* is offset from the exact saddle.

source
QAtlas.@register вҖ” Macro
@register Model Quantity BC method=вҖҰ reliability=вҖҰ tested_in=вҖҰ references=вҖҰ notes=вҖҰ

Thin macro around register!. Lets each model file register its native fetch methods declaratively, e.g.

@register TFIM Energy{:total} OBC method=:bdg reliability=:high \
    tested_in="test/models/test_TFIM_thermal.jl" \
    references=["Pfeuty 1970"]

The three positional arguments are spliced as types; the remaining key=value pairs are forwarded as keyword arguments to register!.
